## [江苏近期将受卢碧台风外围影响](https://m.weibo.cn/search?containerid=100103type%3D1%26t%3D10%26q%3D%23%E6%B1%9F%E8%8B%8F%E8%BF%91%E6%9C%9F%E5%B0%86%E5%8F%97%E5%8D%A2%E7%A2%A7%E5%8F%B0%E9%A3%8E%E5%A4%96%E5%9B%B4%E5%BD%B1%E5%93%8D%23&isnewpage=1&extparam=seat%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot%26dgr%3D0%26cate%3D0%26pos%3D42%26realpos%3D42%26flag%3D1%26c_type%3D31%26display_time%3D1628092916%26pre_seqid%3D1628092916831036186108&luicode=10000011&lfid=106003type%3D25%26t%3D3%26disable_hot%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot) `社会` 
 8月4日上午，南海热带低压加强为今年第9号台风“卢碧”，虽然“卢碧”离江苏还比较远，但近期影响我们的偏东气流，也有它的功劳哦。
## [张常宁说被郎导看中是我的幸运](https://m.weibo.cn/search?containerid=100103type%3D1%26t%3D10%26q%3D%23%E5%BC%A0%E5%B8%B8%E5%AE%81%E8%AF%B4%E8%A2%AB%E9%83%8E%E5%AF%BC%E7%9C%8B%E4%B8%AD%E6%98%AF%E6%88%91%E7%9A%84%E5%B9%B8%E8%BF%90%23&isnewpage=1&extparam=seat%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot%26dgr%3D0%26cate%3D0%26pos%3D47%26realpos%3D47%26flag%3D0%26c_type%3D31%26display_time%3D1628092916%26pre_seqid%3D1628092916831036186108&luicode=10000011&lfid=106003type%3D25%26t%3D3%26disable_hot%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot) `体育` 
 张常宁在19岁时被郎平选进国家队，谈起这段经历张常宁在节目《百年百冠》中说：“能够被郎导看中是我的幸运。” 张常宁也用实力回报了郎平的信任。
## [汕头将有暴雨到大暴雨](https://m.weibo.cn/search?containerid=100103type%3D1%26t%3D10%26q%3D%E6%B1%95%E5%A4%B4%E5%B0%86%E6%9C%89%E6%9A%B4%E9%9B%A8%E5%88%B0%E5%A4%A7%E6%9A%B4%E9%9B%A8&isnewpage=1&extparam=seat%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot%26dgr%3D0%26cate%3D0%26pos%3D48%26realpos%3D48%26flag%3D1%26c_type%3D31%26display_time%3D1628092916%26pre_seqid%3D1628092916831036186108&luicode=10000011&lfid=106003type%3D25%26t%3D3%26disable_hot%3D1%26filter_type%3Drealtimehot) `社会` 
 4-6日汕头有一次暴雨到大暴雨，局部特大暴雨降水过程，沿海陆地风力可达6～8级阵风9级；汕头附近海面风力逐渐增大到8～9级阵风10级。汕头市气象台8月4日9时30分将台风蓝色预警信号升级为黄色，请注意做好各项防台工作。
